[30;1m16 | [0m[35m    On demand distance-based spatial weights-like class.[0m
[30;1m17 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m18 | [0m[35m    Mimic the behavior of ``libpysal.weights.DistanceBand`` but do not compute all[0m
[30;1m19 | [0m[35m    neighbors at once; only on demand. Only ``DistanceBand.neighbors[key]`` is[0m
